\Hypertarget{class_carbon_1_1_carbon_a529169c1bbe05f696b3abce30a51f82a}\index{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon@{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon}!create@{create}}
\index{create@{create}!Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon@{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{create()}{create()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_carbon_1_1_carbon_a529169c1bbe05f696b3abce30a51f82a} 
static Carbon\textbackslash{}\+Carbon\+::create (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$year}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$month}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$day}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$hour}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$minute}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$second}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$tz}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Create a new \doxylink{namespace_carbon}{Carbon} instance from a specific date and time.

If any of \$year, \$month or \$day are set to null their now() values will be used.

If \$hour is null it will be set to its now() value and the default values for \$minute and \$second will be their now() values.

If \$hour is not null then the default values for \$minute and \$second will be 0.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}

\hline
int | null & {\em \$month} & \\
\hline
int | null & {\em \$day} & \\
\hline
int | null & {\em \$hour} & \\
\hline
int | null & {\em \$minute} & \\
\hline
int | null & {\em \$second} & \\
\hline
\textbackslash{}\+Date\+Time\+Zone | string | null & {\em \$tz} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{class_carbon_1_1_carbon_a2653a75fe1a1f5c017a15a8feb2143e2}\index{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon@{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon}!createSafe@{createSafe}}
\index{createSafe@{createSafe}!Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon@{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{createSafe()}{createSafe()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_carbon_1_1_carbon_a2653a75fe1a1f5c017a15a8feb2143e2} 
static Carbon\textbackslash{}\+Carbon\+::create\+Safe (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$year}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$month}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$day}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$hour}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$minute}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$second}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$tz}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Create a new safe \doxylink{namespace_carbon}{Carbon} instance from a specific date and time.

If any of \$year, \$month or \$day are set to null their now() values will be used.

If \$hour is null it will be set to its now() value and the default values for \$minute and \$second will be their now() values.

If \$hour is not null then the default values for \$minute and \$second will be 0.

If one of the set values is not valid, an \textbackslash{}\+Invalid\+Argument\+Exception will be thrown.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
int | null & {\em \$year} & \\
\hline
int | null & {\em \$month} & \\
\hline
int | null & {\em \$day} & \\
\hline
int | null & {\em \$hour} & \\
\hline
int | null & {\em \$minute} & \\
\hline
int | null & {\em \$second} & \\
\hline
\textbackslash{}\+Date\+Time\+Zone | string | null & {\em \$tz} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{class_carbon_1_1_carbon_a83b588b20824e88e5cd2e8ad3790bb1a}\index{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon@{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon}!diffForHumans@{diffForHumans}}
\index{diffForHumans@{diffForHumans}!Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon@{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{diffForHumans()}{diffForHumans()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_carbon_1_1_carbon_a83b588b20824e88e5cd2e8ad3790bb1a} 
Carbon\textbackslash{}\+Carbon\+::diff\+For\+Humans (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$other}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$absolute}{ = {\ttfamily false}, }\item[{}]{\$short}{ = {\ttfamily false}, }\item[{}]{\$parts}{ = {\ttfamily 1}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Get the difference in a human readable format in the current locale.

When comparing a value in the past to default now\+: 1 hour ago 5 months ago

When comparing a value in the future to default now\+: 1 hour from now 5 months from now

When comparing a value in the past to another value\+: 1 hour before 5 months before

When comparing a value in the future to another value\+: 1 hour after 5 months after


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
\doxylink{namespace_carbon}{Carbon} | null & {\em \$other} & \\
\hline
bool & {\em \$absolute} & removes time difference modifiers ago, after, etc \\
\hline
bool & {\em \$short} & displays short format of time units \\
\hline
int & {\em \$parts} & displays number of parts in the interval\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{class_carbon_1_1_carbon_ad1d273c08f892adf6211e4b458b58e87}\index{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon@{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon}!setTestNow@{setTestNow}}
\index{setTestNow@{setTestNow}!Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon@{Carbon\textbackslash{}Carbon}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTestNow()}{setTestNow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_carbon_1_1_carbon_ad1d273c08f892adf6211e4b458b58e87} 
static Carbon\textbackslash{}\+Carbon\+::set\+Test\+Now (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$test\+Now}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Set a \doxylink{namespace_carbon}{Carbon} instance (real or mock) to be returned when a "{}now"{} instance is created. The provided instance will be returned specifically under the following conditions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A call to the static now() method, ex. Carbon\+::now()
\item When a null (or blank string) is passed to the constructor or parse(), ex. new Carbon(null)
\item When the string "{}now"{} is passed to the constructor or parse(), ex. new \doxylink{namespace_carbon}{Carbon}(\textquotesingle{}now\textquotesingle{})
\item When a string containing the desired time is passed to Carbon\+::parse().
\end{DoxyItemize}

Note the timezone parameter was left out of the examples above and has no affect as the mock value will be returned regardless of its value.

To clear the test instance call this method using the default parameter of null.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
\textbackslash{}\+Carbon\textbackslash{}\+Carbon | null & {\em \$test\+Now} & real or mock \doxylink{namespace_carbon}{Carbon} instance \\
\hline
\textbackslash{}\+Carbon\textbackslash{}\+Carbon | string | null & {\em \$test\+Now} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
